I really don't want to go inside due to the pandemic so I wait a full 20 minutes before I go inside and by this time I'm pretty mad. I tell him I went through the drive thru half an hour ago, and his time is so bad that I need a refund now.  At this point the guy drops a brick and literally sprints to get my food out to me. It also turns out that the chow mien was already there and another item had run out while they were waiting. < Review>
I have not been here in years but this place is just as good as I remember. They even added a lift for the handicapped individuals who want to bowl and I thought that was cool. This place is welcoming and you really have no reason not to have a good time here, unless you're by yourself. They also have billiards and arcade games here as well. The food is what you would expect. The public prices are reasonable, and some of the shoe rentals are very old and some are newer but both work. There were plenty of bowling balls when I went but if multiple Lanes were filled there might've been a shortage but not by much. I also observed that the scoring was a bit off at times. We brought a child and he was able to use the bumper lane and the other bowling helper. I am glad that I finally made it back to this alley.</Review>

Whitney Malzhan<//name>
<date>1481574598190<//date><Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
I worked in a veterinary clinic for 6 years and I am very impressed with the patient (and owner) experience Mission Animal Hospital provides.  They have taken excellent care of our aging dogs (currently 14, 14, and 12 years old).

Our beagle has had a weeping tumor removed from behind his ear several times in the past, and I have had other vets tell me it is no longer operable.  Due to his age, I didn't really want to put him through another surgery anyway.  One of the vets at Mission Animal Hospital recommended a holistic approach and we started him on Transcend (a dietary supplement).  After a few weeks of him taking it, I noticed the tumor started to shrink and was not as weepy.  We are now on our second bottle, and although the tumor is still there, it is much more manageable, and is about 1/3 the size it was when he started taking the supplement.

I appreciate the thoroughness of the evaluations and the open-minded approach I feel the vets have taken with my dogs.  I like that they offer holistic options alongside modern medical procedures.  It's like the best of both worlds!  Thank you Mission Animal Hospital!<//review>

<user>109255052974534759895< /user><time>1374023137263<//time><pictures>None</pictures><Rating>5</Rating><text>One of my favorite things that Kevin says is, "We can disagree and still be friends." Being a pretty darn opinionated person when it comes to the health care of any member of my family, this statement was very much appreciated.

Right from the beginning it was clear that this vet was unique in his approach (the entire medical community should take a lesson!). By referring to himself as Kevin, rather than Dr Toman or Dr Kevin, he shows respect for his customers by putting himself on an equal level with them. A subtle difference in language, and yet significant in effect.

His examination rooms have windows, so you can be assured you haven't been forgotten. The open ceilings on these rooms allow you to hear everything he's telling the person in the next room. This lets you get to know him and his approach to pet health care before he even enters your room. After he walks in and introduces himself, he'll sit on the floor and ask you to tell him about your pet. And then he listens. All arrogance and ego have been shed, which allows everyone to focus on doing what's best for the health of your pet.

He is a confident and skilled veterinarian, who is willing to be honest about the limitations of his knowledge and abilities. When I asked him about the value of a certain alternative treatment, he had no problem using those three words that most other doctors seem to avoid like the plague..."I don't know." He said he didn't have any knowledge or experience with that course of action, so couldn't advise on it. That response was totally refreshing.

When I brought our nearly 15-year-old poodle, Booboo, to see Kevin for the first time just a couple of months ago, I knew I was presenting him with a very challenging situation. Booboo had advanced congestive heart failure, severe spinal arthritis, dental disease, cataracts that made him virtually blind, and significant deafness - and those were just the things we knew about. Booboo's time with us was coming to a close, and we knew it. Kevin worked with us to help make Booboo more comfortable, until it became clear that it was time to let him go.

The whole way along, Kevin treated our entire family with compassion, honesty, and respect. Kevin and his staff helped to make a very difficult situation bearable. I wish we had found Kevin sooner in Booboo's life, but since that wasn't possible, I am at least thankful we found him at all.< /text>< Response>

Well, despite not being able to understand anything the person booking our early morning airport pick up said, I went against my gut feeling and hired them. We have two kids, and a 6 am flight, so we arranged them to come at 3:45 am. They said no problem. Asked if I needed car seats - I said no - we had some already, so no need. They told us $60. Seemed a little steep, but hey, it's an EARLY pick up.

I got a call the day of our flight at 2:55 AM! ...asking if they could pick us up at 3:30 am instead of 3:45. Not thinking I had any other option for airport transportation at that point, I said fine. They showed up late anyway. Upon entering the cab, there were two car seats installed. We were surprised and said that it was nice to not have to deal with installing them, even though we were taking them with us. We arrived at the airport making good time...but then we were shocked when he told us the total! He said it was $60, plus $10 for each car seat used, in addition to a $10 card fee, so $90!!! I have had ONLY POSITIVE, HELPFUL, PROMPT RETURN CALLS to questions,  & EXCELLENT PRODUCTS!!!
I read EVERY review prior to going there .. YOU HAVE TO GO & SEE & GET "YOUR" OWN REVIEW .. EVERYONE is different & some people can critique EVERYTHING & EVERYONE RIDICULOUSLY overkill & petty. So please .. ALWAYS keep an open mind & experience for YOURSELF & do not use OTHERS OPINIONS as your own.
I can only say from my EXPERIENCE & my FAMILY who I also sent there & (we come from out if town to SHOP HERE!!) ...You will find extremely clean friut stand, BEAUTIFULLY displayed items, constantly staff freshening the products & EVERYONE was courteous & MOST HELPFUL. If you have any questions .. they are eager to answer or will CALL PROMPTLY to get you answers!!
I am very impressed & will Continue, to drive quite aways, to  give my business to them.
Thank you Loretelli & Family & Employees for your respect, courtesy & appreciation of myself & my family as customers.
Myrna Butler<//Review>

< Text>
We ordered pizza, salad, and soda for delivery. The amount of time until the delivery guy arrived was fine but it went down hill pretty quickly from there. We ordered online and there was one choice for drink size- 20 oz. When the guy showed up he had a 12 oz. can of soda but they charged me for a 20 oz. I asked about that and the delivery driver said they were out of 20 oz. so they replaced it with a can. Wouldn't you think they would have stated that in advance, discounted the bill, or not charged at all? No, instead the response was "yep, we should tell people in advance, thanks." Salad dressing ramakin was barely half full, and the was no forks provided for the salad. These things on their own are no big deal BUT together show a lack of respect for your customers intelligence. As a side note, the pizza was mediocre at best. Crust quickly became cardboard like. I will order from this place again.<//Text>

< Review>
I am a big eater! Of course being a 6 foot man, I can take a lot down. Just because I love to eat, doesn't mean I will eat anything. I have good taste because I know what real good food tastes like.

I came here for the first time with my wife yesterday and I even joined yelp for it. My wife loves to yelp and talked me into starting up so I thought this was the perfect place to review.

I had the lasagna and it was one of the best ones I have had. I love hefty portions and you definitely will not be able to finish this in all one sitting although I got pretty close.

The sauce is very rich and has some great flavors and the meat is seasoned well. My favorite part would have to be the cheese. I'm not sure which ones they use but they work very well with the lasagna.

I want to go out and try something else so if anyone else has any suggestions, I would be more than happy to hear them.< /Review>
